電影專刊

中國電影演員簡論（中）

— 丹楓

至於趙丹和鄭君里二位，我們知道都是由舞台到銀幕極有成績的天才演員，特别是趙丹，更是明星公司最會做戲的小生。再加之他們二人都有很好的學問修養，對社會有着深切的認識，當然是前途遠大無窮，謹在此爲他們祝福。但是消息來，鄭君是在給一個善吃辣椒的女人弄得昏頭昏腦，從前所熱心幹的事，現在一槪置之度外。而趙丹仁兄也在單戀着一個新發現的舞台演員，這樣一來，不能不爲之擔憂。寄語二君，大好前途，千萬别在我愛你你愛我聲中輕輕斷送了。而演技上的比較，那末趙丹是更多方面一些的，鄭君里却以「人生」的典型最成功。另一方面，同樣也以小生資格上銀幕的，如何非光，蔣君超，龔稼農，孫敏諸人，都個别的有其介偶然的成績，而後二人較爲遲鈍一些。唯有張振鐸却眞是無可誇獎，他雖然是那般年紀，但有時還是小生扮裝哩，這是難於理解的了。假使可能的話，他應當扮裝中年而完全放棄文明戲的成分。

無可否認的，生活糜爛，不學無術，乃是一部份演員失敗的致命傷。特别是有些女演員，更染着這一通病。我們不必像煞有介事的指明誰淸白，誰又不淸白，我們也不必因着某人過去的品行不端而作爲蓄意攻訐的焦點，不過事實俱在，眞正希望自已長進的電影演員、應當從私人生活上改善，祇有這樣才能杜絶别人的口實，方能使自已不致被人目爲被玩弄的女性，也祇有這樣才能成爲完全的社會人以及求得演技上之進展。可不是嗎？女演員所以被人們看不起，目爲娼妓同等，所以有人喊着跳出黑暗的電影圈，所以謠傳着誰是台基，誰是達官貴人的外婦，難道不是她們自招侮辱嗎？雖然我們也承認，在現社會中，頗有姿色的女人，要想做一個完人，要想不做商品而不出賣肉體，的確不是一椿容易的事。然而給千萬觀衆所嘱望的女演員，到底得覺悟的潔身自愛，爲了自已的前途，就使生活得淸苦一點，也是很有意義的。（未完）

影片談評

評「大富之家」

— 凌鶴

ＴｈｅＨｏｕｓｅｏｆＲｏｔｈｓｃｈｉｌｄ

丨南京丨（一）

據說，這是一部歷史影片，也是二十世紀公司認爲本年度最偉大的出品。所謂歷史劇自然是根據於歷史的某一葉而編製的劇本，然而某一葉歷史在今日能被採爲電影之題材，决不是一椿偶然的事。譬如說在目前的中國，假使將秦始皇的虐政，以至於陳勝吳廣的揭竿起義，作爲電影的題材，决不是沒有價値的。而歷史的片段，在通過了劇作者的世界觀之後，拿破崙大戰當時的歷史，能反映在「大富之家」的電影中來，一定有其時代的意義。所以，我們對於「大富之家」决不應當因其爲歷史的記載便忽視劇作者觀念的檢討，正相反，祇有這樣才是作品之本質的批判。

（二）「大富之家」所叙述的故事是這樣的：

在猶太人街中，那裏有一羣襤褸的猶太人。他們在黃昏的時候，便被一道鐵練的網封鎖，和猶太人街以外的地方隔離着，不能和外人相往來。

這一羣上帝的選民是被人們輕視着的，成爲下賤的民族，同時就在人們所認爲汚穢齷齪的生活中，我們看見一個老頭兒藏匿着他的錢，告訴他的兒子們怎樣保守他的錢，當官吏來敲詐時候，他們是怎樣裝扮爲窮酸。······也許這便是所謂嗇吝的猶太人之素描罷。直到他臨死的時候，他敎給他的五個孩子怎校樣增加財產的利潤，並且成爲爭奪自由平等之手段。丨丨這算是序曲。

接上我們便看見這Ｒｏｔｈｓｃｈｉｌｄ的錢莊分佈了全歐洲的各地，他們已經擴大了他們父親的資財，而當拿破崙掃蕩歐洲的時候，每一個錢莊所在地的高級官憲，都在向他們借欵，以作爲抵抗拿破崙之軍費。這時英國大將威靈呑也到了倫敦的「大富之家。」就由於他們兄弟的借　，恊約國征服了拿破崙并且將他放逐到巴爾幹　上去了。但是他們所希望的猶太人的自由平等，終於沒有得到，而且猶太人的家屋被人們擲着石塊。甚至於威靈呑所告訴南丹的公債投標，也沒有獲得勝利。直至拿破崙又從关島逃走了以後，整個的歐洲又像陷在地震中的一般驚恐。於是恊約國的政治家將軍們又得求助於這猶太人之家，並且答允了他們要求保障自由平等的條件。到後來南丹露德蔡諸兄弟，冒着極大的危險。直至滑鐵鑪大戰之後，拿破崙再敗，而主人公南丹也受了英國皇家之男爵的封位，猶太人的姑娘也能與威靈呑部下之大將結婚了。

（三）在這故事中告訴我們一些什麽呢？猶太人是愛好和平的，猶太人在大戰中發了財，猶太人因接濟恊約國之軍餉而獲得了爵位，猶太人在拿破崙敗後便獲了自由平等之待遇了。這些是否全是歷史之眞實的記載，我們不必在此置辯，而劇作者的認識，却在此表白了。假使有錢的猶太人可以拿出錢來，打擊歐洲的覇主，便可以抬高他們的地位。但是拿破崙敗後，是否就是眞正的和平呢？而且他們援助軍餉，是否就是爲了和平的奠定呢？與其說是爲了公理或正義，到毌寗說是大富翁戰事的投機吧。敎育錢人犧牲自已的一切來維持和平，這在事實上無論如何是不多見的。至於說從他們手中來獲得民族的自由平等，更是難能可貴的事了。不過他們有錢人却因着軍事投機而買得了爵位，到是我們可以相信的，但這决不是民族解放。

進一步說，歐洲大戰之中，有不少人因軍事投機而發了財，但是德國的戰敗並不是世界的和平。雖然戰後也有一個短時期的資本主義之穏定，可是這一時期早已過去，現在是新的動力在不住的生長，而第二次大戰也快要爆發在目前。所以眞正的和平，决不是建築在少數人身上。

因此，在這裏所表現出來的劇作者的意識，是包含着某種煽動的。至於或許有人說，這是德希特勒驅逐猶太人的反應，也許在這裏頗有附會的可能，果如此，是否就是敎被驅逐着的猶太富翁，帮助軍事野心消滅獨裁政治的德國，而打擊希特勒的國家主義呢？這是我們所不懂的。

總之，我們對於這一影片，决不可相信劇中的唆示，而認爲那是同情弱小民族解放的作品，相反的，他們的解放，無非是富翁們的解放。卽就目前來說，猶太富翁在歐洲握着金融界之絶大勢力，而另一方面猶太民族的勞苦大衆，却始終是毫無國土的在歐美各地操着下賤的苦役，不平等待遇，始終像鐵練一樣繞住着他們的全身。

然而在國家主義跋巵的目前，猶太富翁必然因着民族的關係而被另一民族所排擠，這在德國特别表現得至爲明顯。所以如敎掌握金融之樞紐的猶太人，帮助恊約國消滅正在跋巵着的德國野心家，有如消滅當年的拿破崙一樣，不是毫無原因的；在軍縮會議不能得着他們所想像的效果的當時。這是製片者的政治野心，但是所謂世界和平，却無論如何是一種可怕的欺騙。

（四）至於說這一影片爲什麽對於英國那般表示好感的？那我們當然不能忽視歷史之根據，因爲威靈呑的成功，確實得力於露德蔡不少。又如蘇彝士運河之英國的收買，也是露德蔡一家拿出錢來的。何况亞立斯和卡洛夫諸人都是英國人。

（五）我們從整個的作品來說，在自首至尾劇的發展上，劇作者是極聰明的充分的維持了他的主張，很難看到他意識的矛盾。譬如說他要那富翁南丹向政治當局提出自由平等之要求，而迫着他們簽字，首先便敎我們看見他們自已的家庭也遭受人們石塊的抛擲，使南丹兄弟深感有平等待遇之必要；雖然另一方面，我們也看到他在公債投標的當時，因着那班政治家的操縱而沒有操着勝算。一直到最後爲止，他都自然的將故事發展下去，以至英庭的大受封，而勝利的結論了他的主張。另一方面，南丹的女兒之嫁給英軍官，雖然在劇中只佔着一小部份，但是不能通婚以至於高攀大將，却是强調了劇的主題的。

（六）同樣，自導演以至於表演，都是非常勝利的成功了的。從每一塲面之劇的成份的十分充實，以致於劇的ＴＥＭＰＯ之把握，都顯出電影藝術在現階段中之最高發展。也許有人說當寫到英倫之外的其他四兄弟之支店時，導演運用着完全相同的手法，不免覺着笨拙，然而這是一種不當的評語，因爲旣然不能讓一個故事分四條綫平均發展下去，那末就得極簡潔的聚中在一條主綫上，而完全運用省略法將其餘枝節略去，所以那種採用同樣的方法，正是一種大膽而合理的嘗試。

至於喬其亞理士和卡洛夫的表演技術，直是達到了爐火純靑的地步，不，甚至於那個做南丹兄弟之母親的也是十分成功的。我們簡直可以這樣說，每一個不重要的配角，都有恰到好處的成績。假使我們要看現代電影之藝術，特别是表演技巧，那我們認爲這一「大富之家」，乃是値得十分注意的了。

（七）再還要說到的，便是佈景或攝影收音成功，幾乎是我們用不着在此特别稱讚的，反正在　大的資本之下，這些都是無可否認的做到了。

不過却有人完全給這「偉大」二字迷惑了，非批判的接受作品的全部。所謂「一個弱小民族的反抗，同時向世界作和平之呼籲，以完成了······電影的使命，」這種大膽錯誤的論調，應當是我們所指斥的。

合歡杯」之三主角（左）史本塞屈山（中約）電影小說「三姊妹明星公司出品李萍倩導演（一）」  小榮　　主演····胡蝶嚴月閒林莉孫敏趙丹等　　（一）嬾洋洋的秋天來到，枯黃的樹葉已脫離樹枝了，一陣陣瑟瑟的寒風，呼呼地吹來把這世界平添了幾分的秋意。就在這時，名畫家吳雲林，辭别這冷酷的世界，扔下他老年的妻子，和他三位可愛的女兒，以及幾百張生前精心的傑作，而悄悄的死去了。　　爲了哀悼和紀念這位名畫家，他的家人心及他的學生，替他開了一個「遺作展覧會」。並出售其作品，那天在塲照料的除去他三個女兒，靜芬（胡蝶）瑞芬（嚴月閒）淑芬（林莉）外，還有他的學生趙喧（趙丹）馬一滄（孫敏）等。　　那位紳士派的學生馬一滄（孫敏）望着一張漂亮女子的畫像，心裏便默默的想：「這位女子是多麽的美麗啊！但可惜這張並非是賣品」，他便低低的問靜芬「這張照片可以賣嗎？」　　「呵」！靜芬聽了這話，她似乎難住了，沉思了一刻，便說：「呵！那要去問我的母親呀！」　　「那麽我只好明天到你府上來和師母商量了」。　　第二天的淸晨，這位紳士派的大學生，駕着八汽缸别克汽車，來到了靜芬的家裏商量的結果，吳母終不肯售，原因這是她妹妹的一張遺像。但一滄亦無可如何旋見這間屋子裏一切都似乎是凌亂的，他用着和靄的情調，側了頭很親暱的問道：「看他們這模樣，是不是要搬家呵」？　　吳母苦笑着，點點頭：「對的！沒有房子，正在爲難呢」！　　聽了這話，一滄側過頭來望那美麗的三姊妹，才說；「師母，說也胃昧，不知尊意如何？我有一新别墅倒還空着呢」。吳老師母還客氣着，可是一滄又說道：「你老人家别客氣呀」！我們是師生的關係呀」！「三姊妹」亦慫慂着道；「母親，就搬去吧！」　　這年老人終於敵不過一滄再三的要求，和三位女兒的慫慂，他畢竟是應允了。　　他們遷入新居了。這三位天眞而又活潑的姊妹，在紳士派的馬一滄的眼簾中，都是安琪兒，尤其是那幽靜而溫柔的大姊妹靜芬，更是忚腦膜内終日所愛的一個。於是在某一天他問道：「Ｍｉｓｓ吳，能够允許我給你寫一張肖像嗎？」靜芬說：「那芬說：「那要等我和母親商量後才可以呵！」　　第二天，靜便將這話和他的母親商量，母親一口應允了。瑞和淑亦讚助了。突然那窮小子趙喧跑來了。他聽見了這件事就發表意見道：「我自還是少和他來往的好！先生在世一提起他，便要痛駡的」！（未完）　　小說「海枯石爛」因續稿未到暫停數日

1934.06.14

Five Days Missing, Found on Mountain, Died. On the 8th, He Failed to Send Arishima Off on the Train, Climbed a Mountain, and Hid in a Small Hole Under a Wild Soybean Tree in Ming Xiaoling. Yesterday, He Was First Discovered by Wei Zongqing, a Worker in the Mausoleum Garden.

Nervous Breakdown, Suicidal Intent

Taken Back from Suma to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs

(Nanjing) Deputy Consul Kuramoto of the Japanese Consulate General was safely found around 1:00 PM on the 13th. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 13th)

(Nanjing) Regarding the Incident of Japanese Deputy Consul Kuramoto, Plainclothes Police Searched the Suburbs. On the 13th, a Squad from the Special Police Division of the Police Department Went to Ming Xiaoling and Other Places, Searching Strictly. They Received Reports from Villagers That a Suspicious Person Had Been Wandering in the Mountains for Several Days, Wearing a Suit, Seeming Not to Be a Local. The Police Went to the Back Mountain of Ming Xiaoling and Searched Deeply. They Indeed Found a Person Leaning Against a Tree, Looking Extremely Weak. They Took Out a Photo of Mr. Kuramoto to Compare and Knew That He Was Indeed Kuramoto Himself. Therefore, They Devised Various Plans to Help Him Down the Mountain and Hired a Car Back to Nanjing. It Was a Little After 2:00 PM. They Went Directly to the Police Department, Where Director Chen Zhuo Met Him. Director Chen Had Known Mr. Kuramoto for a Long Time. They Shook Hands and Wept. Director Chen Advised Him to Eat Some Milk, Biscuits, Etc. Kuramoto Was Very Grateful and Drank Two Cups of Milk and a Cup of Soda. Mr. Kuramoto Gave the Following Account: On the Evening of the 8th, I Originally Wanted to Send Ambassador Arishima Off, But There Were Not Enough Seats in the Car (He Wept as He Said This), So I Didn't Send Him Off. I Personally Took a Rickshaw Out of Zhongshan Gate, Along Zhongshan Avenue. Before Reaching Zhongshan Mausoleum, I Turned Into a Mountain Path and Went Up Zijin Mountain. Arriving at the Mountain, I Looked at Nanjing City. The Lights Were Brightly Shining. I Bided Farewell to Nanjing. (He Raised His Right Hand to His Forehead.) There Was a Wooden Frame There. I Nailed My Photos and Business Cards to the Frame as a Memorial. I Had Never Been to Zijin Mountain Before. I Thought There Must Be Many Huge Beasts on the Mountain. At That Time, I Was Lying Under a Tree When I Suddenly Heard the Sound of a Leopard, Coming Closer and Closer. I Took Off My Clothes and Buried Them in the Ground as Food. The Reason for Taking Off and Burying My Clothes Was, First, to Give Convenience to the Leopard, and Second, to Leave No Trace. However, the Leopard Came and Went Several Times, But Never Appeared. The Next Day (the 9th), I Was Very Thirsty on the Mountain, So I Went Down the Mountain to Find Water to Drink. There Was No Spring Water to Drink in the Zixia Cave and Ming Xiaoling Area of Zijin Mountain. That Evening, I Was Still on the Mountain. The Next Day (the 10th), I Was Very Hungry and Thirsty. I Went to a Teahouse Down the Mountain Once to Drink Tea. I Intended to Dig a Big Hole to End My Life, But Because I Had Been Fasting for a Day, I Was Too Weak. So, on the Morning of the 11th, I Went to a Small Noodle Restaurant Down the Mountain and Ate a Bowl of Noodles. When I Went, I Only Had a Couple of Silver Coins Left. Later, I Took Off a Gold Button from My Clothes and Gave It to the Teahouse as Payment, But the Teahouse Didn't Accept It, Saying That Since I Had Forgotten to Bring Money, I Could Pay It Back Next Time. I Don't Want to Talk About the Meaning of This Trip. (He Shed Tears as He Said This.) I Don't Want to Make It Public After Returning to the Consulate. I Originally Didn't Want to Return to Nanjing, But Because the Personnel of Your Department Were Very Sincere, I Was Moved, So I Came Back With Them. At That Time, I Thought to Myself, My Survival or Death Has Nothing to Do With the Empire or Your Country. Now That I Have Returned, Your Country Owes Me Nothing, and I Owe Your Country Nothing. Don't Ask Me Why I Did This. I Don't Want to Say. (He Shed Tears as He Said This.) Then, Director Chen Advised Him to Rest a Little. Mr. Kuramoto Sat on the Sofa, Frequently Raising His Hand to His Forehead. Around 3:00 PM, Shen Jinding, Director of the Asian Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Li Dijun, Director of the Intelligence Department, Gu Zhenglun, Garrison Commander, Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, and Xu Peigen, Director of the General Staff Headquarters, All Heard the News and Visited the Police Department. All of These People Knew Kuramoto and Comforted Him Together. Around 4:00 PM, Shen Jinding Accompanied Him to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and Then to the Japanese Consulate. The Strange Mystery That Had Been Widely Reported in Chinese and Foreign Newspapers for Days Had Come to an End. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 13th)

(Nanjing) Since 9:30 AM on the 9th of This Month, After Being Notified by Personnel Sent by the Japanese Consulate General That Deputy Consul Kuramoto Was Missing, the Police Department Immediately Began a Strict Search at 12:00 PM That Morning. Police Were Dispatched for Several Days, First to the Most Complex Residential Areas in Nanjing and Places Where Foreigners Frequently Visited, Conducting a Thorough Search, But to No Avail. Then, They Turned to the Suburbs and the Areas Along the Jingwu Road Under the Jurisdiction of the Riverside Police Stations, Strictly Ordering the Subordinate Police Stations to Search Separately. Starting on the 12th, They Instructed the Police in Each District With Search Standards: (1) Those With Suspicious Behavior, (2) Those Who Don't Speak the Local Dialect, (3) Those With Strange Appearance, (4) Those Who Seem to Have Mental Illness. All Should Be Noticed, and a Large Reward Was Offered to Ensure Discovery. At 9:00 AM on the 13th, They Received a Call From Zhang, a Local Resident Near the Mausoleum Garden, Requesting That They Send Personnel Quickly, Saying That He Had Important Information to Report. They Immediately Instructed Zhang to Wait in Front of the Tomb in the Mausoleum Garden and Sent Personnel to the Designated Location to Meet Zhang. According to Zhang, Someone Came This Morning to Ask for Water to Drink. The Person Was About 40 Years Old, of Medium Height, With a Small Mustache, Wearing a Semi-New Western Suit. After Drinking the Water, He Walked Slowly Up the Mountain Alone. The Personnel Went to the Mountain Behind the Mausoleum Garden to Search According to This Clue. Around 11:00 AM, They Found a Person Under Zijin Mountain Behind Ming Xiaoling. His Appearance, Build, and Age Were Similar to Those Described by Zhang. He Looked Spiritless, With Disheveled Hair and a Dirty Face. When Asked His Name and Origin, He Was Evasive and Hesitated to Speak. The Personnel, Because He Was Suspicious, Took Out the Photo of Kuramoto That Had Been Prepared in Advance and Compared Them With Each Other. They Felt That They Were Very Similar, and Then Knew That He Was Undoubtedly Kuramoto. They Sincerely Told Him About the Government's Order to the Military Police to Search After the Deputy Consul Left, and Invited Him to Go Down the Mountain and Get Into a Car to Enter the City. Kuramoto Initially Seemed Negative and Refused the Request. After Repeated Persuasion, He Finally Got Into the Car. It Was a Little After 2:00 PM When They Entered the City. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 13th)

(Nanjing) At Noon on the 13th, Kuramoto Eimei, the Japanese Deputy Consul Stationed in Nanjing, Was Discovered by Our Police and Military Police on Ming Xiaoling Mountain. He Was Immediately Escorted Into the City to the Police Department, Where He Was Greeted by Director Chen. Personnel Were Then Dispatched to Escort Him to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Where Suma, the Japanese Consul General Stationed in Nanjing, and Arayano, a Counselor at the Japanese Embassy, Picked Him Up and Took Him Back to the Consulate. According to Reports, Kuramoto Took a Rickshaw Out of the City Alone on the Evening of the 8th and Climbed the Mountain, Attempting Suicide Unsuccessfully. At Noon on the 13th, After Kuramoto Was Escorted to the Police Department by the Police and Military Police, Mai Jiayan, a Reporter From the China United Press, Bi Fanyu, an American Minister, and Zhao Minheng, a Reporter From Reuters, Went to Comfort Him and Inquire About the Details. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 13th)

(Nanjing) According to Another Source, the Reasons Why Kuramoto Was Mentally Disturbed and Had Suicidal Thoughts Were as Follows: (1) Kuramoto Has Been in the Japanese Diplomatic Service for More Than 20 Years, But He Is Still a Deputy Consul, Feeling Frustrated. (2) Ambassador Arishima Came to Nanjing This Time, and Kuramoto Was Not Included in the Japanese Consulate's Banquet, Which Made Him Extremely Angry. (3) When Sending Ambassador Arishima to Shanghai, Kuramoto Prepared Luggage for the Ambassador, But Could Not Get a Seat in the Car. His Nerves Received a Great Shock, and He Was Angry and World-Weary. Another Saying Is That Kuramoto Had a Quarrel With His Wife Before Leaving. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 13th)

(Nanjing) Confirmed News. The Reason for Kuramoto's Suicide Was Due to His Personal Pessimism and Weariness of the World. The Detailed Reason Is Being Studied. Some People, Because His Suicide Action Was So Peculiar, Questioned Him, Saying, "If You Want to Die, Just Die. Why Do You Have to Hide Like This?" Kuramoto Said, "After I Climbed the Mountain, I Was Afraid That Wild Animals Would Come and Harm Me. I Once Wanted to Commit Seppuku, But I Didn't Bring a Sword, and I Didn't Have Money to Buy a Knife, So I Couldn't Do It." When Asked Why He Didn't Think of His Life's Work When He Thought of Committing Suicide, Kuramoto Said, "I Was Really in Great Pain. I Had to Say Goodbye to the World." When Asked Why He Didn't Think of His Children, Kuramoto Said, "There Is No Need to Worry About Children. It's Like a Tree Has Already Sprouted. Why Worry That It Won't Grow Up?" When Asked If He Didn't Think of His Beloved Wife, Kuramoto Said, "My Wife Is Not Enough to Stop My Suicidal Thoughts." When He Was Told That Since the News of His Disappearance Spread, His Old Mother in Japan Had Been Crying All Day Long, Didn't He Think of This? Kuramoto Knelt Down, Raised His Hands to the Top of His Head and Pressed Them Together, Repeatedly Saying "Amitabha Buddha," Tears Streaming Down His Face, and Cried Bitterly. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 13th)

(Nanjing) After Deputy Consul Kuramoto Was Found by the Police Department on the 13th, the Director of the Asian Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Shen Jinding, Was Notified to Go to the Department to Talk With Mr. Kuramoto. Director Shen Immediately Went to Meet Mr. Kuramoto, First Comforting Him, Then Asking About the Situation After His Disappearance, and Its Reasons and Motives. Mr. Kuramoto Did Not Want to Say the Reasons and Motives, and Said That Without the Consent of the Consul General, He Would Not Make It Public. He Only Described His Experiences in the Mountains, and Also Talked About and Drew a Diagram of Where He Hid and Stayed. The Following Is What Mr. Kuramoto Said in Response: "I (Kuramoto Self-Described) Intended to Depart This World on the Evening of the 8th. I Originally Planned to Send Ambassador Arishima and Other Secretaries to the Station to Say Goodbye, But Because There Were Not Enough Seats in the Car, I Gave Up and Let My Colleagues and Guests From Shanghai Go. I Originally Wanted to Go to Qixia Mountain, But Because the Train Time Was Not Suitable, I Changed My Destination to Zijin Mountain. The Local Staff Had All Gone to Xiaguan. I Left the Consulate at About 10:45 PM and Hired a Rickshaw Separately, Asking Him to Pull Me to Outside Zhongshan Gate. When the Rickshaw Arrived at Zhongshan Gate, the Rickshaw Puller Refused to Leave the City Because It Was Too Late. I Got Out of the Rickshaw in Front of Zhongshan Gate and Walked Out of the City. I Walked to the Top of Zijin Mountain, Looking Down at the City. I Saw the Electric Lights Shining Brightly. I Was Filled With Emotions. I Put My Hands Together and Said Goodbye to All My Relatives and Friends in the City. At That Time, I Had Realized Everything. After Saying Goodbye, I Climbed the Triangular Tower on Zijin Mountain. When Climbing the Tower, I Took a Few Business Cards and Photos From the Business Card Holder, Tied Them With a Handkerchief, and Hung Them on the Handrail of the Triangular Tower as a Sign That I Had Been Here. I Spent the Night on the Mountain That Evening. I Suddenly Encountered a Large Wild Animal, Similar to a Leopard or a Large Wildcat. I Had Already Decided to Commit Suicide, So I Didn't Have to Worry About Being Chewed to Death by It. I Was Only Afraid That If I Was Bitten to Death by a Wild Animal, My Clothes Would Definitely Be Left in That Place and Easily Discovered by People. I Took Off My Clothes and Buried Them in the Ground, Waiting Quietly for It to Attack. Unexpectedly, This Beast Chased Other Small Animals Elsewhere. Then, I Thought That Being Bitten to Death by a Wild Animal Was Not Worth It, So I Lodged on a Pine Tree, But the Large Wild Animal Never Came Again. The Next Day, I Went Down the Mountain. Then, Because I Wanted to See the Beautiful Scenery of the Sunrise, I Climbed the Mountain Again. At This Time, I Was Very Hungry, So I Walked to Zixia Cave to Drink Water. Last Night, I Spent the Night on a Large Tree Near Zixia Cave. There Were Also Many Wild Animals Near That Place, But I Was Still Safe and Sound, and I Felt Very Happy Instead." (At This Time, Director Shen Took Out a Slip of Paper and Asked Him to Draw a Diagram and Dates.) Kuramoto Continued, "Until the 10th, I Went From Zixia Cave to the Back Mountain of Zhongshan Mausoleum. At That Time, I Planned to Fast and Die Here. So, I Planned to Move Stones to Build a Place to Die. However, There Were Too Few Stones in That Place to Build a Grave. On the Evening of the 10th, I Spent the Night on a Large Tree in That Place. On the Evening of the 11th, I Went From Zhongshan Mausoleum to the Back Mountain of Ming Xiaoling. I Also Moved Stones in That Place and Started Building a Grave Again. However, Because That Place Was Close to the Edge of the City and There Was a Small Road, I Was Deeply Worried That After I Died in That Place, the Corpse Would Smell Bad and Be Easily Discovered by People. Therefore, I Changed My Plan Again and Walked Further Into the Mountains. I Found a Cave. This Cave Seemed to Be a Nest of Wild Animals. I Modified This Cave a Little and Hid in It. However, Until the 12th, Because of Intense Hunger, I Slinked Out of the Cave to Drink Water Again. On the Evening of the 12th, I Returned to the Cave to Spend the Night. Today, I Was So Hungry That I Couldn't Bear It Anymore, So I Went Out of the Cave Again and Went to a Teahouse in Front of Ming Xiaoling to Drink Tea. At That Time, There Were Only Two Mao Coins in My Pocket. I Paid the Teahouse Fee. However, Because I Was Very Hungry, I Ate Noodles Again, So I Gave a Pair of Gold Buttons to the Teahouse Landlady. She Said That What I Ate Was of Very Little Value and Refused to Accept It, Saying That I Could Wait Until Next Time. I Replied That I Might Not Come Again, So I Gave This Button to a Nearby Worker, Asking Him to Buy Chicken Eggs for Me. I Went Back to the Cave to Rest. However, the Nearby Residents Already Knew That I Was Hiding in the Mountains, So They Searched the Mountains Extensively and Were Finally Discovered by Them. The Above Is the Situation After I Left the Consulate on the Evening of the 8th Until I Was Discovered. I Regret That I Went Out of the Mountain to Find Food and Drink, Which Caused the Residents to Be Suspicious." (Central News Agency Dispatch, 13th)

(Nanjing) After Kuramoto Went Missing, the Military Police Worked Day and Night to Investigate. On the 13th, They Found Him in a Place Rarely Visited. It Is Said That the Government Will Give Him an Award. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 13th)

(Nanjing) Japanese Deputy Consul Kuramoto Was Found by Our Military Police Near Ming Xiaoling Outside Zhongshan Gate on the 13th. He Was Immediately Taken Into the City, First to the Police Department for a Brief Interrogation. Kuramoto Originally Went Out to Commit Suicide. At 4:15 PM, the Department Sent Police Officers to Escort Kuramoto to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. On One Hand, the Ministry Notified the Japanese Consulate by Phone. At 4:30 PM, Japanese Counselor Arayano and Consul General Suma Came to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Person. At 5:05 PM, They Took Kuramoto Back to the Consulate. According to Reports, Kuramoto Intended to Commit Suicide Because He Was Reprimanded by His Superior for Official Business, So He Angrily Went to Ming Xiaoling. Kuramoto Lived in a Mountain Cave About Three Li From the Mausoleum. On the Afternoon of the 11th, He Went to the Shunxing Store No. 1 in Mingling West Village and Ate a Bowl of Ham Noodles, Two Chicken Eggs, a Plate of Melon Seeds, a Pot of Tea, a Pack of Great Britain Cigarettes, and a Bottle of Beer, Worth a Total of One Yuan and Forty Wen. Because He Had No Money, He Wanted to Leave His Western Shirt and Gold Cufflinks With the Store Owner Liu Fengxiang. Liu Told Him That If He Had No Money, He Could Send It Over Tomorrow. Kuramoto Said That It Didn't Matter and That He Would Bring the Money Tomorrow to Pick It Up. So, He Put Down the Gold Cufflinks and Left. At That Time, Liu Did Not Suspect That He Was Japanese Because Kuramoto Spoke Fluent Chinese. (Special Dispatch, 13th)

(Nanjing) An American Newspaper Reporter Went to the Japanese Embassy to Collect News About Kuramoto's Disappearance. According to What He Told People Afterwards, the Embassy Staff Said at That Time That After Returning Home, Kuramoto Himself Said That His Hiding Was Entirely Due to "Family Matters and Too Slow Promotion." Kuramoto Did Not Admit That He Planned to Commit Suicide. According to Kuramoto, After Leaving the Japanese Embassy on Friday Evening, After Sending Japanese Ambassador Arishima to Shanghai, He Hired a Rickshaw to Dongmen and Sneaked Into the City, Not Noticed by the Garrison. Then, He Climbed Zijin Mountain Behind Xiaoling, Looking at the Sleeping City From Afar, Raising His Hand Over His Head and Waving and Calling Out, "Goodbye, Everything, Everything." When Describing This, Someone Asked Why He Hid. Kuramoto Said Excitedly That He Only Wanted to "Escape." It Is Said That He Hastily Started to Build a Windbreak That Evening, Piling Up Stone Walls. During These Days, Kuramoto Was on the Mountain. At Night, He Moved Stones to Build a Windbreak. During the Day, He Leisuredly Traveled at the Foot of the Mountain. The First Person to Discover Him Was a Farmer, At One O'Clock in the Afternoon. He Was Lying in This Small Hut. The Farmer Reported to the Police Station, and Kuramoto Was Taken to Headquarters.

After Kuramoto Arrived at the Police Station, He Stayed for a Very Short Time. At This Time, He Was Questioned by the Staff, and He Declared That His Disappearance Was Automatic, Because He Lost Some Official Documents Last Week and Was Reprimanded by His Superior, Which Was Inevitably Embarrassing. According to Kuramoto's Appearance, Although He Was Very Exhausted, There Were No Obvious Difficulties or Physical Abnormalities. When the American Newspaper Reporter Went to the Police Station, Kuramoto Could Say His Name. The Same Was True for the Personnel of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. He Said That He Felt Nothing But Hunger in His Stomach. When Asked If He Felt Happy About Returning to the City Now, Kuramoto Strenuously Said That He Did Not Want to Return and Said, "My Return Is Very Inappropriate." When Asked What He Planned to Do With His Wife and Children, He Said Casually, "They Have Their Own Way of Surviving." Looking at Kuramoto's Intention, From the Police Station Back to the Japanese Embassy, There Was No Special Interest. At 5:00 PM This Afternoon, He Was Handed Over to Suma, the Japanese Consul General, at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and Taken Back to the Japanese Consulate. Japanese Newspaper Reporters in Nanjing Are Still Not Allowed to Visit Kuramoto in the Japanese Consulate Because the People in the Consulate Said, "He Is Too Weak to Work Again." However, It Is Said That When Kuramoto Was on Zijin Mountain, He Went to the Foot of the Mountain to Buy Food, So He Did Not Seem to Be Physically Weak. In Addition, Foreign News Said That the Japanese Side Will Order Kuramoto to Send a Letter to Our Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Express His Apologies. (Special Dispatch, 13th)

(Nanjing) After Central News Agency Reporters Learned That Kuramoto Was Found, They Immediately Bought a Car Out of the City to Explore Where He Was Hiding. When They Arrived at Ming Xiaoling, There Were Still Dozens of Police Officers Patrolling There, Everyone With a Tired Look on Their Faces, But Now With Happy Faces. When Asked Where Kuramoto Was Hiding, They Said That It Was Behind the Mountain, and It Would Be Difficult to Reach All Day Without Someone to Guide Them. At the Ming Xiaoling Sacrificial Hall, They Saw an Officer of the Military Police Headquarters, Leading a Bare-Chested Man, Preparing to Enter the City. This Person Was Wei Zongqing, the Mausoleum Garden Worker Who First Discovered Kuramoto. The Reporters Climbed the Mountain Led by Zhang Qihe, a Staff Member of the Mausoleum Garden, Climbing Up the Mausoleum. The Road Was Only Wide Enough for One Person, With Random Stones Protruding. They Walked for About a Li to the Top of the Tomb and Went Down Again. Wild Grasses Were Luxuriant and There Was No Road to Find. They Pushed Through the Grass and Advanced. After a Long Time, Under a Wild Soybean Tree, They Found Where He Was Hiding. This Place Was a Small Hole, Only Enough to Accommodate a Person's Body. The Head Had to Be Exposed Outside the Hole. The Hole Was Surrounded by Wild Soybeans and Wild Grasses, Like a Wild Animal's Nest. Kuramoto Took Leaves and Flattened the Bottom of the Hole and Lay in It. Kuramoto Had Another Cave for Resting During the Day, One Li Away, Also in a Place Rarely Visited. Our Military Police Finally Discovered It. Their Diligence and Hard Work Can Be Seen. Kuramoto Had Been Hiding for Five Days, Looking Haggard, With a Worried Look on His Face All Day Long, Looking Down With His Eyes, As If Unable to Bear the Sighs. He Needed Someone to Help Him Walk, Unable to Lift His Feet. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 13th)

(Nanjing) Central News Agency Reporters Learned That the Person Who First Discovered Kuramoto on the Morning of the 13th Was Wei Zongqing, a Mausoleum Garden Worker. Because Kuramoto Had Been Living Alone in the Mountains for Several Days and Was Extremely Thirsty, He Went Down the Mountain to Find Water on the Morning of the 13th and Met Wei. Kuramoto Spoke Very Fluent Chinese. They Talked to Each Other. Wei Bought Four Chicken Eggs for Kuramoto to Fill His Stomach. After a While, Zhang Qihe, a Staff Member of the Mausoleum Garden, Saw the Situation and Also Went to Investigate, Suspecting That It Was Kuramoto. He Urgently Reported to the Military Police by Phone, and Kuramoto Was Found. Wei Zongqing Is From Suxian County in Southern Anhui, 33 Years Old, and Usually Works in the Mausoleum Garden, Earning a Few Corners of Wages a Day. He Has Now Been Taken to the Headquarters by the Military Police and Will Be Rewarded. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 13th)

(Nanjing) According to Reliable Sources, Kuramoto Went From His Residence to the Consulate at 10:30 PM on the Evening of the 8th, Intending to Go to Xiaguan to Send Arishima to Shanghai. Because the Car Was Full, He Did Not Get His Wish. Then, He Hired a Rickshaw, Reached Zhongshan Gate Along Zhongshan Road, and Gave the Rickshaw Puller a Silver Coin of Two Corners. Then, He Walked Up the Mountain Alone. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 13th)

(Nanjing) Mr. Kuramoto, the Japanese Deputy Consul Who Went Missing Last Friday Evening, Was Found Asleep in the Forest Under Zijin Mountain Around 2:00 PM Today. The Finders Were Four Detectives. Mr. Kuramoto Was Mentally Disturbed. Because He Had Been Sleeping Outdoors for Several Days, He Was Quite Tired, But His Health Was Still Good. After Being Awakened by the Detectives, Kuramoto Initially Did Not Want to Return to Nanjing. After Repeated Persuasion, He Agreed to Return. It Was 3:00 PM. The Police Department Treated Him With Food. At 4:00 PM, a Reuters Reporter Went to See Him. Kuramoto Spoke Very Fluent Chinese and Described in Detail the Situation After His Disappearance, Saying That After 10:00 PM on the Evening of June 8, I Was at the Japanese Consulate General Preparing to Go to Xiaguan to See Japanese Ambassador Arishima Off, But the Car Was Very Crowded, So I Hired a Rickshaw and Went Along Zhongshan Road to the Mausoleum Garden. I Arrived at Zhongshan Gate at Midnight. The Rickshaw Puller Was Unwilling to Go Forward, So I Waved Him Away and Walked Out of the City. The Gatekeeper Did Not Stop Me. The Reuters Reporter Asked Him the Reason for This Strange Action. Kuramoto Initially Did Not Want to Say, But Then Said That When I Walked Out of Zhongshan Gate That Night, I Felt a Strange Feeling of Happiness and Satisfaction. I Walked Past the Mausoleum Garden and Climbed Zijin Mountain. I Looked Down at Nanjing From the Top of the Mountain and Saw the Electric Lights Flickering. I Waved My Hand and Said Goodbye to China's Beautiful Capital. The Wind on the Mountain Was Strong, Especially That Night. I Piled Up Stones to Build a Temporary Dwelling for Myself. I Did This Every Night. I Was Originally Determined to Abandon the World. Unfortunately, I Drank Water. Otherwise, I Wouldn't Be Here Now. The Reuters Reporter Told Him That Nanjing Was Very Happy to Hear That He Was Safe. Kuramoto Replied, "I Am Not Happy. Everyone Has Different Views on Life." The Reuters Reporter Told Him That His Wife and Children Would Be Happy to See Him Return. Kuramoto Replied, "They Can Take Care of Themselves." The Reuters Reporter Asked Him If He Was Hungry. Kuramoto Replied That He Did Not Feel Hungry After the Police Department Provided Him With Food. After the Conversation, Kuramoto Shook Hands With the Reuters Reporter to Say Goodbye. The Handshake Was Strong, But His Fingers Were Slightly Wet, Which Proved That His Nerves Were Not Calm. (Reuters Dispatch, 13th)

(Nanjing) After Jin Bin, the Director of the Police Department, and Fan Hansheng, the Section Chief of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Accompanied Kuramoto to Get Out of the Car at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, They Were Invited to Rest in the Reception Room of the Permanent Vice Minister. Zhu Hexiang, the Director of the International Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Li Dijun, the Director of the Intelligence Department, and Li Shengwu, the Director of the General Affairs Department, Entered the Room One After Another to Comfort Kuramoto. Because They Were Old Acquaintances, They Shook Hands One by One to Thank Him. At That Time, Fang Zhi, the Secretary of the Central Propaganda Committee, and Xu Enzeng of the Central Organization Committee Also Came to the Ministry to Visit. Afterwards, Shen Jinding, the Director of the Asian Department, Notified the Japanese Consulate General by Phone, Asking Consul General Suma to Come to the Ministry. Soon, Consul General Suma and Secretary Arayano Came to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Meet. Vice Minister Tang Youren and Director Shen and Others Invited Kuramoto to the Great Reception Room to Meet Together. When Kuramoto Saw Suma and Arayano, He Burst Into Tears. Suma and Arayano Comforted Him. Vice Minister Tang Also Expressed His Condolences. Afterwards, Vice Minister Tang Asked If He Took a Rickshaw Out of the City on the Evening of the 8th. Kuramoto Replied That, According to Japanese Language, He Went by Rickshaw. Later, Vice Minister Tang Asked What Time It Was. Kuramoto Replied That It Was About 12:00 PM on the Evening of the 8th, When He Arrived at Zhongshan Gate. At That Time, Consul General Suma Said, "He Seems Tired Now. Let's Talk Less." Vice Minister Tang Asked Again, "Is Your Spirit Good Now?" Kuramoto Replied, "It Is Gradually Getting Better Now." Soon, Japanese Newspaper Reporters Miyazaki, Okano, and Takahashi, and Wang Jianrong of the China Photo Studio Entered the Room to Take Pictures of Kuramoto. After Taking Pictures, Arayano and Suma Urged Him to Return to the Consulate Immediately. At 5:20 PM, Consul General Suma and Secretary Arayano Accompanied Kuramoto Back to the Japanese Consulate General. Shen Jinding, Li Dijun, Li Shengwu, Zhu Hexiang, and Fan Hansheng of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Sent Him to the Gate and Said Goodbye by Raising Their Hands. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 13th)

(Nanjing) After Kuramoto Was Accompanied Back to the Japanese Consulate From the Ministry of Foreign Affairs by Suma, Arayano, and Others to Rest for a While, the Consulate Sent Personnel to Send Him Back to His Residence at No. 62 Yinyangying to Meet With His Wife Reiko. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 30th)

(Nanjing) After the Japanese Consul Kuramoto Went Missing, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Notified the Military Police Authorities to Do Their Best to Search for Him for Several Days. He Was Found by the Police Department in Ming Xiaoling on the 13th and Escorted Back to the Department. A Document Was Prepared to Send Personnel to Escort Him to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Informing Consul General Suma to Come to the Ministry to Verify and Retrieve Him. The Military Police Headquarters Also Prepared a Document Reporting That Deputy Consul Kuramoto Intended to Commit Suicide and There Was No Other Reason. In Addition, the Cufflinks That Mr. Kuramoto Gave to the Small Noodle Restaurant Have Also Been Found by the Military Police and Sent to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 13th)

(Nanjing) Kuramoto Had Lunch at Liu Fengxiang's Shunxing Teahouse No. 1 in Mingling West Village on the Afternoon of the 11th. Central News Agency Reporters Visited the Store's Housewife on the Afternoon of the 13th. According to the Conversation, a Man Came to the Store for Lunch on the Afternoon of the 11th and Ate Tea, a Bowl of Ham Noodles, Two Chicken Eggs, Bought a Pack of Great Britain Cigarettes, a Pack of Melon Seeds, Worth a Hundred Wen, and Left at 4:00 or 5:00 PM. Before Leaving, He Bought a Bottle of Beer, Totaling One Yuan and Four Copper Coins. But He Did Not Bring Any Money and Wanted to Leave His Western Shirt and Gold Cufflinks as Collateral. We Firmly Refused, Saying That He Could Pay It Next Time. But He Insisted on Leaving It. When He Left, He Said That He Would Come Again Tomorrow. Because He Spoke Chinese Very Fluently, We Did Not Pay Attention. Now, the Military Police Department Has Sent Personnel to Take the Cufflinks Away to Be Stored in the Department. In Addition, Those Who Went to the Police Department to Comfort Kuramoto From Our Authorities, Besides Chen Zhuo, Were Gu Zhenglun, Chu Minyi, Xu Enzeng, Shen Jinding, and Fan Hansheng. When Kuramoto Arrived at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, He Rested on the Second Floor. Tang Youren Also Came to Comfort Him. At 5:05 PM, He Took the Japanese Consulate's Car No. 1132 Back to the Japanese Consulate. When Going Downstairs, Because He Was Extremely Tired, Suma Supported His Left Arm, and Arayano Supported His Right Arm Downstairs. The Staff of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and Reporters Stood By and Watched. Many People Were Watching. Shen Jinding, Li Shengwu, Li Dijun, and Fan Hansheng Sent Him to the Gate and Waved Goodbye. In Total, From His Disappearance at 10:30 PM on the Evening of the 8th to His Discovery at About 11:00 AM on the 13th, It Was 110 Hours. The Reward of Ten Thousand Yuan Offered by the Military Police Will Be Distributed to the Search Teams of the Two Departments, the Military Police, the Mausoleum Garden Guards, the Nearby Residents, and Those Who Have Contributed. Wei Zongqing, the Worker Who First Discovered Him, Will Also Receive a Large Reward. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 13th)

Case of a Student Studying in Japan Being Brutally Murdered: Japanese Side's Evasive Words; Light Punishment for the Murderer Watanabe

Nagasaki: The Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Tokyo made an unofficial announcement on the 12th regarding the brutal murder of Ye Muhua, a Chinese student studying in Nagasaki. However, the truth is as follows: On May 20th, at 12:25 PM, three students from the private Nichika Commercial School in Higashiyamamachi, Nagasaki City, were playing soccer in the street in front of the school. At that time, Ye Muhua, a Chinese student from Fuzhou, residing at 27 Shinchi, Nagasaki City, aged 19, was passing by. Watanabe Tatsuo, a student from the school, accidentally kicked the ball at Ye, and the two began to argue. Watanabe stabbed Ye in the chest with a short knife, and Ye immediately lost consciousness and died. The police arrested Watanabe and, after a thorough interrogation, punished him. However, the reason was that the two had been on bad terms for some time, and Ye insulted Watanabe, leading to the act of violence. However, this is merely a children's quarrel, completely different from the Kura Moto incident where a diplomat disappeared in the capital. (13th Dispatch from Dentsu)

The Future of the German and Italian Prime Ministers' Meeting

— Respectfully

After the heads of state of Italy, Austria, and Hungary met in Rome, the situation in Europe suddenly changed. The slogan of economic cooperation was merely a superficial gesture; its actual effect lay in political understanding. In other words, it was to establish the foundation for Italy's hegemony in Central Europe. Germany, unable to fully succeed in Austria and failing to achieve its wish to tear up the Treaty of Versailles, and with its eastward expansion blocked by the united efforts of the Soviet Union and France, found itself in a diplomatic dilemma. Unwilling to condescend to return to the League of Nations, yet unable to fully exploit the contradictions among continental European nations to forge its own path, German diplomacy fell into a quagmire from which it was difficult to escape. Among European countries, only Italy shared similar interests and viewpoints with Germany. Before the understanding among Italy, Austria, and Hungary was established, an understanding between Italy and Germany would not be difficult, and even a joint effort against France was possible. This was because Italy was also dissatisfied with the Treaty of Versailles and had long advocated for reforming the League of Nations. Since the rapprochement between France and the Soviet Union, Germany had faced increasing restrictions on all sides, making Italy and Germany more inclined to approach each other. First, Italy and Germany were both anti-League of Nations forces, unwilling to let Britain and France control everything, and wanting to re-evaluate the balance of power in Europe. It was clear that if Germany could break free from the constraints of the treaty, Italy could use this to share hegemony in Central Europe and even expand its influence in North Africa. Although Italy and Germany had different fundamental positions, they shared the goal of destroying the shackles of the League of Nations. Second, Italy's army was not weaker than France's, but in terms of new weapons, especially the equipment of the air force and the foundation of mechanical industry, Italy could not compete with France. Its natural resources were also very scarce. Without strong external support and skillful use of diplomatic conflicts, it would be difficult for Italy to maintain its status as a major power. Germany, seeing the compromise between France and the Soviet Union and Britain's superficial observation, had to insist on its claim of equal military strength to encourage its national courage and enhance its international status. Italy, unable to compete with France, wanted to use Germany's strength to help itself. This was another reason why Italy and Germany could negotiate an agreement. With these two reasons, the two dictators had today's meeting in Venice. We do not need to predict the specific content of the talks, as the general idea can be gleaned from previous consultations among the three countries. Apart from the above two points, it is difficult to form a more powerful action to break the current situation in Europe.

The reason Austria abandoned its kinship with Germany in terms of race and language and became close to Italy was that the German National Socialist Party was too reckless, causing embarrassment to figures like Dollfuss. At the same time, Germany was unable to provide Austria with a maritime outlet, causing its economic panic and hindering its early recovery. This led to the understanding among Italy, Austria, and Hungary, creating a semblance of an economic alliance. If the meeting between Mussolini and Hitler does not involve political and economic issues, it will be fine. However, if it touches on political and economic relations, the Austrian-Hungarian question will immediately become a current obstacle, further stimulating the sharp opposition between the two extreme nationalistic states. Both want to use Austria as a satellite to compete for hegemony in Central Europe, and with France mediating between them, the problem becomes even more complicated. Regarding relations with the Soviet Union, based on the superficial situation between Italy and Germany, there should not be much conflict. However, today's Germany, unable to actively compete with France, must find a way to break through its surrounding weaknesses to develop its national strength. Therefore, adopting an aggressive stance towards the Soviet Union is almost inevitable. In pure theory, Italy may agree with this, but in reality, would it really want Germany to develop as much as possible? Before World War I, Italy was originally a member of the Allied Powers, but later joined the Entente and became an enemy of Germany. The past serves as a lesson. Therefore, Italy and Germany cannot avoid being wary of each other, especially regarding relations with the Soviet Union. Moreover, since the small countries in the Danube River region expressed dissatisfaction with France, Italy intends to take the opportunity to advance and establish its hegemony in Central Europe. Germany is also eager to get involved and would not allow Italy to dominate alone. This is another factor that prevents Italy and Germany from coordinating. Therefore, the cooperation between Italy and Germany can only break the current situation in Europe to a certain extent, and the rest will still be mutually opposed.

Our Country Implements Factory Law; Concession Authorities Obstruct

Representative Li Submits to the International Labor Organization

Industrial Development Targeted in Four Years

(Geneva) At the meeting of the International Labour Office, Mr. Li, the acting representative of China, stated today while discussing the report of the board of directors that the Chinese government recently intended to implement the Factory Law of 1929 and sent personnel to investigate and supervise the working conditions in factories in the concessions. However, the concession authorities refused, which is a great act of divergence, as the concessions are still Chinese land. Mr. Li also mentioned that the Chinese government has formulated a three-year plan to place unemployed workers in road construction and other projects. The Chinese government also seeks industrial development and plans to implement a four-year plan with 620 million yuan. Five large factories have now been established. (Reuters, 13th)

The Two Ruthless Italian and German Leaders Meet in Venice Today; Heart-to-Heart Talks on Major Issues at the Palazzo Pisani; Austrian Situation and Disarmament are Focuses of Discussion; Hitler Arrives by Plane This Morning; Italian Ships Gather in the Adriatic Sea to Show Respect

Prime Minister Mussolini of Rome and Chancellor Hitler of Germany are scheduled to begin their meeting on the 14th at the Palazzo Pisani in Stra, between Padua and Venice. Most of the Italian representatives participating in the meeting have already departed for Venice tonight. Hitler will come by plane with Foreign Minister Neurath and will arrive on Thursday morning. German Ambassador to Italy Hassell will also participate at that time. Prime Minister Mussolini is currently in Cordenons and will go directly to the meeting place from there. (Havas, 12th)

Note: Venice was a republic from 697 to 1797. This time, when Hitler visits, celebrations will be held here to commemorate the prosperity of the Venetian Republic.

Rome: German Chancellor Hitler will arrive in Venice tomorrow. However, it is generally believed that Italian newspapers are criticizing France's policies in anticipation of his meeting with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. Ten Italian warships have gathered in the lagoon west of the Gulf of Venice to show respect. The two prime ministers will meet at the Palazzo Pisani in Stra, ten miles west of Venice. The mansion formerly belonged to a noble family, and Napoleon once resided here when he drove the Austrians out of the city. In front of it is a large square surrounded by ancient trees. When the two prime ministers discuss world affairs in the mansion, no outsiders will be able to observe them, as police and plainclothes officers will be stationed around the mansion. Hitler will travel with Foreign Minister Neurath and is expected to arrive by plane at 9:30 tomorrow morning. Mussolini and others will greet him at the airfield on the outskirts of the city and prepare a grand banquet to welcome the two guests. In the afternoon and evening, the two prime ministers will discuss everything at the Palazzo Pisani. On Friday morning, the meetings will continue. Italian Undersecretary Suvich will host a luncheon for Hitler and Neurath at the Lido Dance Club at noon. Hitler will host a banquet at his hotel in the evening for Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and others. When the two prime ministers meet, the Italian side will include Undersecretary Suvich, Italian representative to the League of Nations Aloisi, Italian Ambassador to Germany Cerruti, and Fascist Party Secretary Starace. The German side will include Foreign Minister Neurath and German Ambassador to Italy Hassell. Roman authorities remain silent on the issues to be discussed, and newspapers have not carried any news. It is heard that this meeting was initiated by Berlin, and Mussolini only agreed to it when he saw that the Geneva Conference was about to fail. Disarmament and Germany's return to the reorganized League of Nations are certainly on the agenda, but the situation in Austria seems to be a matter of great concern to both sides. Mussolini will advocate that Germany no longer assist the Austrian National Socialist Party, and Hitler seems likely to reiterate that Germany does not want to achieve the union of Germany and Austria by force. (Reuters, 13th)

British Air Force Expansion Plan: Adding 600 Aircraft Within One Year, Training Pilots, and Increasing Squadrons to Compete with France

(London) British Privy Council member Baldwin recently stated that if a disarmament restriction agreement cannot be reached, Britain will try to catch up with the world's largest air force in the shortest possible time. Based on this proposal, the Aviation Department is now planning to expand the British Air Force and will submit it to the Cabinet meeting soon. It is heard that this new plan proposes to increase the number of air force squadrons by 50. In other words, 600 aircraft will be added within one year, 20 new airfields will be added, and the number of aviation personnel will be greatly increased. The UK has 800 first-line aircraft and about 130 second-line aircraft, excluding 100 aircraft in India. If expanded in the future, the UK air force will roughly be able to compete with France. Not Deceived by the Japanese; Mexico Refuses to Recognize the Puppet State; The Estrada Doctrine Does Not Apply

Mexico: The Associated Press correspondent learned today that Mexico has not been induced by Japan and has refused to recognize "Manchukuo". The Estrada Doctrine stipulates that Mexico recognizes friendly countries, regardless of how the country was established. According to reliable sources, Mexican government officials told the Japanese minister that the Estrada Doctrine only applies to established countries, and "Manchukuo", as a newly emerging country, is not within the scope of recognition. The Estrada Doctrine was advocated three years ago by Mr. Estrada, the former governor of Mexico (Estrada is currently the ambassador to Spain). At that time, coups broke out in Central and South American countries, and the situation was turbulent, making Mexico's position difficult. Therefore, the doctrine was advocated. Page 8

The US Once Again Cables Britain; War Debts Can Be Renegotiated; Requests Britain to Submit New Suggestions; and Allows Debt Repayment in Goods

(Washington) The United States delivered a cable to Britain today regarding war debts, requesting that new suggestions be submitted. This shows that the United States clearly wants to reopen all war debt negotiations based on a new position. The cable is only a response to Britain's statement of suspending war debt payments. Secretary of State Hull personally handed it to British Ambassador Lindsay. It states that the United States welcomes Britain's suggestion of paying off debts with goods. Observers indicate that the right to pay off debts with goods may be extended to other debtor nations. If so, the entire war debt problem will be completely changed. Hull said that he had also received a cable from France. Although the content of the cable has not been made public, France has also formally notified its decision to suspend the war debts due on June 15. In his cable to Ambassador Lindsay, Hull said that the United States is very willing to informally discuss any suggestions from the British government. Although there has been no discussion of paying off debts with goods before, such suggestions, if beneficial to both countries, can be discussed at length for submission to Congress for approval. Hull also asked Britain to pay attention to President Roosevelt's message to Congress. Observers here generally believe that the United States' new action is a wise step. The cable will lead to negotiations for the United States to accept British rubber, tin, ingots, and other goods that the United States lacks. Secretary of State Hull and the French Ambassador to the United States are unwilling to criticize the French cable. However, a cable from France stated that the French Cabinet had decided to continue the suspension of payments, so the French cable formally notified the suspension of payments, which is beyond doubt. Belgium and Czechoslovakia also cabled the State Department yesterday, suspending debts due on Friday. (National Telegraph, 13th)

(London) The possibility of repaying debts with goods mentioned in the American war debt message is attracting great attention here, especially because it represents a more conciliatory attitude on the part of the US government. (Reuters, 13th)

(London) Since the American statement on war debts agreeing to accept goods in lieu of cash was released, the stock exchanges yesterday evening and today have shown a marked improvement. The American statement is seen as very important because (1) it contains formal American recognition of the difficulty of repayment, and (2) it offers hope of solving the war debt problem by substituting cash with tin, rubber, manganese, and whiskey. However, this kind of transaction may cause serious disturbances in the foreign exchange market, which will result in (1) a more stable dollar price, which the American authorities do not want, and (2) disrupting the balance of the British imperial currency, as the British government must purchase and sell tin and other goods from various parts of the empire. Some people speculate that due to the above-mentioned difficulties and because Finance Minister Chamberlain believes that Britain's repayment of American war debts should depend on whether various governments repay British war debts, the British government may not be happy with the idea of substituting goods for cash. (Reuters, 13th)

(Paris) The French government's decision to refuse to repay a portion of the war debt owed to the United States when it becomes due on the 15th of this month has been approved by the French cabinet today, and it has been decided to send a cable to Washington tomorrow. However, the press release issued today stated that former Prime Minister Herriot strongly disagreed with the Cabinet's decision, as Mr. Herriot's usual position is that France should repay war debts as usual. (National Telegraph, 12th)

(Paris) The government has prepared an official document regarding the war debt issue due on June 15 this year, which has been telegraphed to the French Ambassador to the United States, de Laboulaye, instructing him to forward it to the US government. The document states that the French government maintains the legal view of the French Chamber of Deputies' decision of December 14, 1932 regarding war debts, that is, since Germany has stopped paying France, France cannot repay debts to the United States either. Since December 14 of that year, although various events have occurred, the French government has always adhered to the view of the French Chamber of Deputies. It is heard that de Laboulaye will deliver this document to the US government before June 15. (Havas, 12th)

Netherlands and Belgium Maintain the Gold Standard

Amsterdam: The National Bank of the Netherlands issued a report today stating that it is necessary to organize an international group to maintain the gold standard. The report warned of the danger of devaluation of the Dutch currency and stated that the Netherlands will devote all its efforts to maintaining the gold standard and is unwilling to make any discussions. International trade has continued to decline since the failure of the World Economic Conference. According to the report, the bank's surplus was 2,669,408 guilders (Dutch currency), while last year's surplus was 1,004,202 guilders. The bank announced a dividend of 32 guilders. Central vs. Local: Spain's Serious Situation - Catalonia to Declare Republic, Central Government to Stop by Force

The situation between the autonomous region of Catalonia in Barcelona and the central Spanish government has become serious due to the new Catalan land law. Today, troops here are gathered in military camps awaiting orders, and public institutions are protected by soldiers. The only topic of general discussion is the possibility of Catalonia declaring a republic. Today, crowds gathered in front of the parliament, shouting "Long live the Republic, Down with the traitors!" The Spanish flag hanging in the parliament has been removed. The president of the Catalan autonomous region addressed the crowd, saying that the central government will use force to prevent the implementation of the new land law. It is reported that the land law recently passed by the Catalan parliament cancels the contracts concluded between tenants and landlords regarding land taxes, etc., which are generally paid by the tenants. This plan was later deemed invalid by the central government's court. As a result, thirty-six Catalan members withdrew from the National Assembly, claiming that if the central government did not change its attitude, they would no longer enter the National Assembly. Catalonia includes the four provinces of Barcelona, Tarragona, Lleida, and Girona. According to the law passed by the Spanish National Assembly on September 9, 1932, an autonomous region can be established within Spain, with a parliament and an executive council, independently managing education, economy, society, and police affairs within the region. (Reuters, 13th)

The leaders of the Spanish constitutional faction in Madrid are striving to extend the life of the cabinet and enable the parliament to continue until December next year. Robert, the right-wing leader who controls the parliament, admitted this to an Associated Press interviewer, saying, "We must do our best to clear the thorns of the current government so that we can form a majority party government in the fall. Only a government supported by the majority party in parliament can solve economic and social problems." Robert believes that the current parliament may not be able to continue until December 1935. Robert indicated that since the right-wing controls the parliament, there is a risk that the parliament will be dissolved at any time. It is heard that Robert will succeed Zapote as Prime Minister. Roosevelt Signs Reciprocal Tariff Act

(Washington) President Roosevelt signed the Reciprocal Tariff Act today. At the same time, Secretary of State Hull issued a statement saying that the act aims to revitalize international trade based on the principle of reciprocity. Hull hopes that international stability can be fully achieved so that all countries can restore past trade. Hull also stated that the act will eventually equalize currencies and improve the international financial structure. Although Hull's statement expressed optimism, it is generally believed here that if there is no hope of breaking the war debt stalemate, the value of negotiating reciprocal tariffs with various countries will be greatly diminished, as the act does not mention the cancellation or reduction of war debts. Therefore, if the United States conducts reciprocal negotiations with debtor countries, the debtor countries will take the opportunity to demand a reduction in war debts. The act authorizes the President to directly negotiate commercial treaties with foreign countries and modify tariffs based on these treaties. According to recent information, the act will reduce taxes on some imported goods, but the President still signed the act. Those affected by the act include automobiles, trucks, foot-operated vehicles, wood, wood products, books, and coal. (National News Agency, 12th)

Procedures for Reporting and Re-exporting Imported Foreign Goods

(Nanjing) The Customs Administration issued an order to customs offices in various places on the 13th: (1) For imported foreign goods for which proof of tax payment cannot be presented, a period of ten years from the date of import of the foreign goods will be allowed to retain the benefit of tax-free re-export. However, after ten years, they should be treated as domestic goods and subject to export tax when shipped abroad, and transit tax when shipped to other commercial ports in the country. (2) Regardless of the time limit, if the original import situation of imported foreign goods cannot be verified when reporting for re-export, but the customs deems the reason stated by the merchant for not being able to verify it is legitimate, it shall be handled in accordance with the prescribed tax collection method; otherwise, it should be rejected according to the regulations. In the absence of tax payment certificates, import tax should be collected. (3) If a merchant who has paid import tax on foreign goods wishes to enjoy the benefit of tax-free re-export within a ten-year period, he must apply for a re-export permit and properly preserve the detailed information about the import of the goods in order to present it to the customs for inspection and verification when reporting for re-export within the time limit for proof. (Special Dispatch, 13th)

Liaoning Farmers Suffer Brutal Persecution

(Tianjin) At the confluence of the Yunhe, Taizihe Rivers in the Xitang Mazhai area of Anshan, Liaoning, there is a levee that was built by villagers who raised funds to prevent the overflowing of river water in summer and autumn from flooding their fields. Water in Tangjiazhuang Mine Gradually Receding

It will be completely pumped out in another week. The workers have all returned to work in the first and second passages to temporarily maintain their livelihoods. (Special Dispatch, 13th)

Zhu Tingfen Commits Suicide in Desperation - Commission Certificate Arrives at Hotel - One Hour Before Hanging

(Jinan) Zhu Tingfen from Henan and Zhang Honglie, the Director of the Construction Department of this province, were fellow villagers. Zhu once served as the Director of the Henan Industry Department. Due to poverty, he came to Jinan this spring to seek a job from Zhang. Yesterday, Zhang finally recommended Zhu as a counselor and supervisor of the Qingdao Salt Affairs Inspection Office. This morning at 8 o'clock, he went to deliver the commission certificate, but Zhu had hanged himself at 7 o'clock on the upper floor of the Tianxiang Inn in the Dongxiang County in the city. Zhu was good at mathematics and had a published work, which had been sent to the Commercial Press for publication. (Special Dispatch, 13th)

Jiangxi Bandits Flee to Southern Anhui and Are Repelled | The Bandits' Strength Is Greatly Diminished, and They Can Be Annihilated |

Wuyuan Correspondence: The bandits who disturbed Qixi Daohu, Liwu, Jiajiawan, and northeast Fuliang were attacked by the two battalions of Jiao and Qu sent by Chen Diaoyuan and the joint brigade of the Tenth District Security. Seeing that it was not easy to attack Qimen, and that their rear was cut off by various armies, the bandits gathered scattered bandits and fled from north Fuliang into the border of Qiupu Zhiedong, three counties adjacent to Qimen, relying on danger and holding on. Xiayu Ban, which belongs to Dongliu County, was once occupied by bandits on the 29th of last month. After Chairman Liu sent a mortar company to encircle and suppress them, the bandits disintegrated and retreated. Xiayu Ban is 40 miles away from Zhiedong County and 75 miles away from Pengze in Jiangxi. The people in the county are panicked. The authorities have sent teams to prevent and block them. According to refugees who escaped from Jiajiawan, the bandits have the flags of the Chinese Communist Propaganda Team and the Chinese Red Army Jiangbei Guerrilla Brigade, both with red ground and white characters, more than 100 rifles, two machine guns, and four submachine guns. Most of the rest are wooden sticks and spears. Their strength is no longer substantial, and it will not be difficult to gather and annihilate them after dispatching troops to encircle and suppress them from all sides. (8th)

Disaster Situation in Hengfeng County | The Provincial Relief Committee Sends Personnel to Inspect |

Hekou Correspondence: Among the counties in eastern Jiangxi that have fallen to banditry, Hengfeng is the most deeply affected. In the winter of the 16th year of the Republic of China, bandits Fang and Shao launched an uprising, and Ge Yuan Town and the county seat were successively lost, and the entire territory was red. Recently, the 21st Army of the National Army recovered Hengfeng County. The Jiangxi Provincial Relief Committee specially sent Min Dingyi, director of the disaster relief receiving center in Shizuo, and special commissioner to inspect the disaster situation in eastern Jiangxi, to Hengfeng to inspect the disaster situation. He arrived in Hekou on May 30. When the Hengfeng County Government heard the news, they sent Tong Section to Hekou to negotiate and expressed their welcome. Inspector Min then went to Hengfeng, passing through villages along the way, inspecting each one in detail. A desolate scene of weeds and broken walls was unbearable to witness. After arriving at the county seat, County Magistrate Xie and Wang Instructor of the 21st Army's Training and Political Office led him to inspect the disaster situation in the urban and suburban areas. The next morning, he went to the disaster victims' homes to express his condolences one by one, and then went to the temporary rehabilitation committee for investigation. Then he went to the 21st Army Headquarters to meet with Commander Liang to discuss the relief situation. He immediately returned to Hekou to report the actual situation of the Hengfeng disaster to the provincial government, the disaster relief committee, and Chairman Wen for instructions. Attached is the telegram as follows: "On the order of this month, I went to Hengfeng from Hekou on the 2nd to inspect the disaster situation. Passing through the villages, the roads were covered with weeds, there were no residents in the houses, and the dilapidated and destroyed state was extremely tragic. After entering the city, the fields and gardens became barren land, and seven or eight out of ten houses were burned. Those who survived had no doors and no walls, and it was impossible to find a table or a chair to rest on. Recently, several refugees have returned and surrendered, mostly with no clothes to cover their bodies and no food to eat, looking emaciated and starving. Hengcheng has just been recovered and has no resources for relief. Even neighboring counties such as Raoyan and Yi are areas affected by banditry and have no time to care for their neighbors. For the sake of appeasing the people, it is necessary to telegraph Your Excellency to allocate relief funds and send personnel to set up a reception center to comfort those who have returned. Otherwise, the refugees will have nowhere to beg and the wandering masses will hear and stop. It is very worrying. Is there anything appropriate? I am waiting for your instructions." (5th)

Sichuan Bandits Surrender, Claiming Internal Disintegration; Inspector Suggests Developing Transportation to Liu Chengfu; the More Transportation is Advanced, the More Difficult Transport Becomes, Sharing Similarities with the Bandit Suppression in Jiangxi; Steady and Solid Progress is the Only Unchanging Principle in Bandit Suppression

Chengdu Dispatch. The military operations to suppress bandits in Sichuan Province are progressing rapidly. Recently, the bandits have been increasingly disintegrating and living in constant fear.

The supplies in Dehan City have gradually moved towards the Bashan Mountains, indicating their intention to flee into the mountains. This shows their final desperate struggle and that they are in their last throes. It is expected that the suppression of these bandits is just around the corner after the start of the fourth phase of the general offensive. Recently, many have returned from the front lines to surrender. From the 3rd Division, 9th Brigade, several bandits, including Qiao Yulong and Yang Fatang, surrendered with their weapons. They claimed that there is a Wangjiaba within the Liangzi Mountains of Bashan, which serves as the bandits' general hospital, housing over ten thousand seriously wounded. The number of lightly wounded is countless. They also stated that the old bandits from other provinces are very wary of the new bandits from Sichuan, prohibiting them from whispering or walking in groups of three. Each guard post has "old countrymen" (口號 - their motto) from other provinces monitoring them. Therefore, the Sichuan people among the bandits are suffering unspeakably, and everyone wants to revolt but lacks the opportunity. Our defection and escape were also fortunate successes. According to what we know, the number of those killed for wanting to revolt is no less than a thousand. This is enough to know that the internal disintegration of the bandits is not difficult to eliminate. However, due to the high mountains and dangerous terrain in the Tongba area, the roads are difficult to travel, and all kinds of transportation are challenging, causing military delays. This is the reason why Inspector Luo Shuchang of the Fifth Route and Inspector Shuzhi of the Sixth Route saw this and telegraphed General Commander Liu Xiang, offering suggestions on developing transportation and preventing bandit conspiracies. Liu Xiang greatly appreciated it. The original text of their suggestion stated, "Transportation is of great importance to the national economy and the people's livelihood. In peacetime, it facilitates the circulation of goods, promotes culture, transmits politics, and prospers the local area. In wartime, it facilitates military transport, quickens the flow of information, supplements military opportunities, and reduces labor costs. The various benefits are truly difficult to fully enumerate. In the recent situation in eastern Sichuan, if there were convenient transportation, then the small area of Tongjiang and Wanyuan would have been swept clean of bandits long ago, gathering and annihilating them. Why would we be constrained and affect progress? Although each route is winning step by step, the more we advance, the more difficult transportation becomes. Despite spending tens of thousands of dollars on labor and materials every day, the army at the front is still struggling to sustain its food supply. This is the same problem as the past failure of bandit suppression in Jiangxi, which was caused by the inconvenience of transportation. For more than a year, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has firmly advocated the principle of steady and solid progress. Whenever a position is captured, transportation is immediately established along with it. The actual benefits are not superficial. Compared to the labor costs of the civilians, it cannot be measured in miles. Moreover, from now on, for ten or a hundred years, the people will forever enjoy its benefits, and the utility of local products is secondary. Sichuan is a land of abundance. All of the province's hundred-plus counties are fertile areas, especially the Tongba area, bordering Shaanxi. The terrain is naturally dangerous. Zhang Xianzhong, Wang Sanhuai, and their ilk successively occupied it to cause chaos in Shu. The historical scars are still there, all because transportation was inconvenient, making it difficult to suppress them, and this contributed to it. It is proposed to instruct the highway bureaus to strive for the development of transportation in eastern Sichuan. The section from Wanxian to Xuanhan should be built quickly to benefit bandit suppression. After the bandits are cleared, the section connecting Tongba should be built. This will solve the problem once and for all, remove obstacles, make it difficult for bandits to hide, and bring endless blessings to the local area for generations to come. It is also heard that the bandits have sent people to instigate our military laborers to riot and to supplement our soldiers to create internal chaos. If this is true, the rear is truly worrying, and the front will also be significantly affected. It is requested to instruct all departments and supply stations to pay special attention, conduct strict investigations and defenses, and carry out party purification work in each county to eliminate hidden dangers. It is also heard that due to the hot weather along the supply lines, porters are dying every day. If more medical personnel can be sent, carrying medicines, to provide timely relief at each supply station, it will prevent the reduction of transportation capacity, and the future will rely on it."

Kailuan Majiagou Coal Mine Labor Strike Occurs; Workers Strike Because Reduced Work Affects Livelihood; Settled After Mediation

Tianjin Dispatch. The Kailuan mines have been troubled in recent years. The Tangshan mine strike almost became unmanageable. Just over a month after it was settled, incidents occurred again at the Tangjiazhuang and Majiagou mines. The Majiagou mine workers went on strike at 12:00 AM on June 8th. The cause of the strike was that the mine bureau reduced workers' working hours to control output and prevent surpluses. The workers went on strike because their income was insufficient to maintain their livelihood, demanding the restoration of the original working hours. Originally, the Majiagou mine had over a thousand workers, producing about 2,300 to 3,000 tons of coal per day. This year, the sales of Kailuan coal outside the pass were affected by the arbitrary imposition of tariffs by the puppet state. Even the Jinxi and Xingcheng areas could not transport coal to within the war zone. Furthermore, due to the intrusion of the puppet Beipiao coal and Fushun coal, the sales along the Yangtze River were also squeezed by the dumping of Fushun coal. Sales were not as good as before. Since spring, there has been a large amount of coal in stock. To avoid surpluses, the mine management specifically controlled production, intending to restore the original production of each mine after the stored coal was sold off, starting with the Majiagou mine. Production was reduced from 2,300 tons to 400 tons per day. The workers were originally contract workers, earning more wages when they produced more coal. Since the amount of coal produced was reduced, their income naturally decreased. The workers calculated that their income was insufficient to maintain their lives. Two days ago, they contacted the labor liaison office newly established by the mine bureau in the mine area, requesting a return to normal. The mine bureau ignored their request and did not reply. By 12:00 AM on the 8th, the workers could no longer endure it and went on strike during the shift change. The order was still good after the strike. The mine inside and outside was protected by the mine area's second security team. The mine bureau was informed the next morning and immediately sent Secretary Zhang Guanru to mediate. Zhang arrived at the mine at 3:30 PM on the 9th. At the same time, Li Yinchun, the resident inspector of the Industry Department in Tangshan, also rushed to the city to mediate with the workers. Apart from the previous request, the workers had no other conditions. Zhang Guanru reported this to the mine bureau. The mine bureau believed that the Tangjiazhuang mine had not fully resumed work, and the Majiagou mine could not have another strike, which would reduce the total amount of coal produced. Therefore, it was handled according to the contract agreement and restored the amount of work that the workers should do. The workers were satisfied and returned to work at 12:00 AM on the 9th. Although a small number of workers did not immediately return to work, it was due to private disagreements with the contractors, not related to the mine bureau. Therefore, in fact, the mine had returned to peace after the strike. The incident at the Tangjiazhuang mine was at the end of last month, when the mine's power generator caught fire, burning the second coal mine. After a week of repairs, coal has been produced. However, production has been reduced by two-thirds. A few days ago, the water pump in the third coal mine suddenly broke, and water poured out like a waterfall, flooding the mine. More than a hundred workers working inside were killed, and dozens were injured. The water in the mine was eight or nine feet deep. Technicians have been supervising the work to pump water out for days, but it has not been completely pumped out. The third coal mine cannot produce coal in a short time. The entire Tangjiazhuang mining area has a total of three tunnels. Now two of them have been destroyed. The coal seam in the first tunnel is almost exhausted, and there is not much production per day. Therefore, the entire mine is currently equivalent to being abandoned, and the mine management has suffered significant losses. (10th)

Songjiang, Sheshan Robbery Injures Neighbors

Robbery cases in the four townships of this county occur from time to time. Yesterday (the 12th) at about 9:00 PM, at the home of Jiang Xinyuan, across the river from the Yejiafen cemetery about half a mile south of Sheshan, suddenly four or five bandits speaking with a Hakka accent arrived, holding firearms. During the robbery, the village dogs barked wildly, alerting the neighbors, who got up to investigate. Knowing that the Jiang family was being robbed, they quickly beat gongs to warn others. The bandits, relying on their guns, were not afraid at all and continued to rob as usual. When Shen Shunzhou and Shen Wang Asan, a woman, went to peep in front of the Jiang family's door, they were seen by the bandits, angering them. The bandits fired shots, hitting Shen Shunzhou in the right waist and his wife in the right arm. They fled in pain, and the bandits chased them but fortunately missed. By the time they got home, they were covered in blood and breathing rapidly. Shen Shunzhou's injuries were severe. After the bandits left, the neighbors gathered to watch and then transported them to Songjiang to receive treatment at the Ruoshe Hospital.

Kunshan, Chief of Public Security Bureau Changes

Hua Shijun, the Chief of the Kunshan County Public Security Bureau, has only been in office for nine months. He has now received an order from the provincial government to be transferred to the province. His vacated position will be filled by Hu Xingbo. After receiving the order, Hua has instructed his subordinates to rush to complete the handover. It is heard that the new Chief Hu is scheduled to arrive in Kunshan on the 20th to take over.

Fire Brigade Members Clash with Patrol Officers

The fire fighting efforts in this county have always been well-developed. The reason is that the members of the fire brigades in each district are all volunteers. Whenever there is a fire, they rush forward bravely. Therefore, the people of all circles have deep faith in the fire brigades. Whenever purchasing equipment, they donate enthusiastically. Therefore, the equipment of the fire brigades in each district is mostly excellent. At 8:00 PM on the afternoon of the 12th, a fire suddenly broke out at the home of Shen Zilan in Houbang due to carelessness. Members of the fire brigades in each district heard the alarm and drove to the rescue one after another. Fortunately, it was extinguished quickly. When the members of the fire brigade in the west district heard the alarm, they were late because of the long distance. The patrol officers blamed them for being late. The members were not convinced, leading to a quarrel. Both sides fought. A member was beaten by a patrol officer, arousing public anger. They dragged the fire engines into the Public Security Bureau. Afterwards, the audience numbered in the thousands, and the voices were boiling. Zhang Ruifu, the inspector of the Public Security Bureau, feared that the situation would escalate and urgently invited Li Jie, the chairman of the Fire Brigade Federation, to the bureau. He asked Li to persuade the members to drag the fire engines back, promising to investigate the patrol officer who caused the incident and punish him severely. After Li's persuasion, the members dragged the fire engines back. Today, the Federation convened a meeting to discuss negotiation methods.
