Film Special Issue

A Brief Discussion on Chinese Film Actors (Middle)

— Dan Feng

As for Zhao Dan and Zheng Junli, we know that both are talented actors who have achieved great success from the stage to the screen. Zhao Dan in particular is the most talented young leading man in the Star Film Company. In addition, they both have good academic backgrounds and a deep understanding of society. Of course, their future is infinitely bright, and I hereby wish them well. However, the news is that Zheng Jun has been infatuated with a woman who likes to eat chili peppers, and the things he used to be enthusiastic about are now put aside. Brother Zhao Dan is also in love with a newly discovered stage actor. In this way, we cannot help but worry. I would like to say to the two gentlemen, do not lightly sacrifice your great future in the midst of "I love you, you love me." As for the comparison in acting skills, Zhao Dan is more versatile, while Zheng Junli is most successful with the "Life" archetype. On the other hand, He Feiguang, Jiang Junchao, Gong Jianong, Sun Min and others, who also entered the screen as young leading men, have individually achieved occasional success, while the latter two are somewhat more sluggish. Only Zhang Zhenduo is really not worth praising. Although he is that old, he sometimes still dresses up as a young leading man, which is difficult to understand. If possible, he should dress up as a middle-aged man and completely abandon the elements of civilization drama.

Undeniably, a decadent life and lack of knowledge are the fatal wounds of the failure of some actors. In particular, some actresses are even more infected with this common problem. We don't have to point out who is innocent and who is not, and we don't have to use someone's past misconduct as a focus for deliberate attacks. However, the facts are all there. Film actors who truly hope to improve themselves should improve their private lives. Only in this way can they prevent others from criticizing them, and only then can they not be regarded as women who are being played with. Only in this way can they become complete social beings and seek progress in acting. Isn't that right? The reason why actresses are looked down upon and regarded as equal to prostitutes, the reason why someone shouts to jump out of the dark film circle, and the reason why it is rumored who is the mistress of a high-ranking official, is it not because they invite insult upon themselves? Although we also admit that in today's society, it is indeed not an easy task for a woman with quite a beautiful appearance to be a perfect person and not to sell her body as a commodity. However, actresses who are expected by millions of viewers must realize that they must cherish themselves and maintain their integrity. For the sake of their own future, it is meaningful to live a hard life. (To be continued)

Film Reviews

Review of "The House of Rothschild"

— Ling He

The House of Rothschild

丨Nanjing丨 (1)

It is said that this is a historical film and that Twentieth Century Fox considers it their greatest production of the year. A historical drama is, of course, a screenplay based on a certain page of history. However, the fact that a certain page of history can be adopted as a film subject today is by no means accidental. For example, in the current China, if the tyrannical rule of Qin Shi Huang, leading up to the uprising of Chen Sheng and Wu Guang, were made into a film, it would definitely not be without value. The historical fragment, after passing through the worldview of the playwright, and the history of Napoleon's great wars, can be reflected in the film "The House of Rothschild," it must have its significance in the times. Therefore, we should never neglect the examination of the playwright's ideas of "The House of Rothschild" simply because it is a historical record. On the contrary, only in this way can we achieve a critique of the essence of the work.

(2) The story told in "The House of Rothschild" is as follows:

In a Jewish neighborhood, there is a group of ragged Jews. At dusk, they are sealed off by a chain-link net, separated from the outside world, and cannot associate with outsiders.

This group of God's chosen people is despised by people and becomes a lowly race. At the same time, in what people consider to be dirty and filthy lives, we see an old man hiding his money, telling his sons how to keep his money, and how they disguise themselves as poor scholars when officials come to extort money... Perhaps this is the so-called sketch of stingy Jews. Until his death, he taught his five children how to increase the profits of their property and make it a means of fighting for freedom and equality. 丨丨 This can be considered the prelude.

Next, we see the Rothschild bank spread across all parts of Europe. They have expanded their father's wealth, and when Napoleon swept across Europe, high-ranking officials in every location of the bank were borrowing money from them to use as military expenses to resist Napoleon. At this time, the British general Wellington also arrived at the "House of Rothschild" in London. Due to the loans from their brothers, the allied powers conquered Napoleon and exiled him to the Balkans. However, the freedom and equality that they hoped for for the Jews were not obtained, and Jewish houses were pelted with stones. Even Wellington's telling Nathan about the public debt tender did not achieve victory. Until Napoleon escaped from the island again, the whole of Europe was frightened as if it were in an earthquake. So the politicians and generals of the allied powers had to turn to this Jewish house for help again, and agreed to their demands for guaranteeing freedom and equality. Later, the Rothschild brothers took great risks. Until after the Battle of Waterloo, Napoleon was defeated again, and the protagonist Nathan was granted the title of Baron by the British Royal Family, and the Jewish girl was also able to marry a general under Wellington.

(3) What does this story tell us? Jews love peace, Jews made a fortune in the great war, Jews obtained peerages for supplying the Allied forces' military expenses, and Jews obtained freedom and equality after Napoleon's defeat. We do not need to argue here whether these are all true historical records, but the playwright's understanding is revealed here. If wealthy Jews can take out money to strike at the European hegemon, they can raise their status. But after Napoleon's defeat, is it true peace? And is their aid to military expenses for the sake of establishing peace? Rather than saying it is for the sake of justice or righteousness, it is more like speculation in the war by the wealthy. Teaching wealthy people to sacrifice everything for the sake of maintaining peace is, in fact, rarely seen. As for gaining national freedom and equality from their hands, it is even more precious. However, we can believe that wealthy people buy peerages through military speculation, but this is by no means national liberation.

Further speaking, in the European war, many people made fortunes through military speculation, but Germany's defeat is not world peace. Although there was a short period of capitalist stability after the war, this period has long passed, and new forces are constantly growing, and a second world war is about to break out. Therefore, true peace is never built on a small number of people.

Therefore, the consciousness of the playwright expressed here contains a certain amount of agitation. As for perhaps someone saying that this is a reaction to Hitler's expulsion of the Jews, perhaps there is a possibility of interpretation here. If so, is it to teach the expelled Jewish tycoons to help military ambition to eliminate dictatorial Germany and strike at Hitler's nationalism? This is something we do not understand.

In short, we must not believe the instigation in this film and think that it is a work that sympathizes with the liberation of small and weak nations. On the contrary, their liberation is nothing more than the liberation of the wealthy. Even in the present day, Jewish tycoons hold the great power of the financial world in Europe, while, on the other hand, the working masses of the Jewish nation have always been without land, engaged in lowly hard labor in various parts of Europe and the United States, and unequal treatment is still wrapped around their entire bodies like iron chains.

However, in the current situation of rampant nationalism, Jewish tycoons are inevitably being squeezed out by other ethnic groups due to ethnic relations. This is particularly evident in Germany. Therefore, teaching the Jews who control the hub of finance to help the Allied powers eliminate the German warmongers who are currently rampaging, just as eliminating Napoleon in those years, is not without reason. At a time when arms reduction conferences cannot achieve the results they imagine, this is the political ambition of the filmmakers, but so-called world peace is, in any case, a terrible deception.

(4) As for why this film shows such goodwill towards England? Of course, we cannot ignore the historical basis, because Wellington's success was indeed due to a great deal of help from the Rothschilds. Also, the British purchase of the Suez Canal was also made possible by the Rothschild family taking out money. What's more, Arliss and Caloff are all British.

(5) From the overall work, in the development of the play from beginning to end, the playwright is extremely clever and fully maintains his proposition, and it is difficult to see contradictions in his consciousness. For example, he wants the tycoon Nathan to make demands for freedom and equality to the political authorities, forcing them to sign, and first teaches us to see that their own family is also subjected to people throwing stones, so that the Nathan brothers deeply feel the need for equal treatment. Although, on the other hand, we also see that at the time of the public debt tender, he did not gain the upper hand due to the manipulation of those politicians. Until the very end, he naturally develops the story to the point where the British court is greatly ennobled, and concludes his proposition with victory. On the other hand, Nathan's daughter's marriage to a British military officer, although it only occupies a small part in the play, the fact that she cannot intermarry to the point of marrying a high-ranking general emphasizes the theme of the play.

(6) Similarly, from the director to the performance, they are all very successful. From the full fulfillment of the dramatic elements of each scene to the grasp of the TEMPO of the play, it shows the highest development of film art at the current stage. Perhaps some people say that when writing about the branches of the other four brothers outside of England, the director's use of the exact same technique is inevitably clumsy. However, this is an inappropriate comment, because since it is not possible to let a story develop evenly along four lines, then one must concentrate very concisely on one main line and completely use the method of omission to skip the remaining branches. Therefore, the adoption of the same method is a bold and reasonable attempt.

As for George Arliss' and Boris Karloff's acting skills, they have truly reached the point of perfection. No, even the actress who played the mother of the Nathan brothers was very successful. We can simply say that every unimportant supporting role has just the right achievement. If we want to see the art of modern film, especially acting techniques, then we believe that this "House of Rothschild" is worth paying close attention to.

(7) What remains to be said is that the success of the scenery or photography and sound recording is almost something we do not need to praise here specifically. Anyway, under the enormous capital, these are undeniably achieved.

However, some people are completely confused by the word "great" and accept the entirety of the work uncritically. The so-called "the resistance of a small and weak nation, while at the same time appealing to the world for peace, in order to fulfill the mission of film," this bold and erroneous argument should be what we criticize.

The Three Protagonists of "The Cup of Joy" (Left) Spencer Tracy (Center) Movie Novel "Three Sisters Star Company Production Li Pingqian Director (1)" Xiao Rong Stars: Hu Die, Yan Yuexian, Lin Li, Sun Min, Zhao Dan, etc. (1)

Lazy autumn has arrived, the withered yellow leaves have fallen from the branches, and gusts of cold wind are blowing, adding a bit of autumnal mood to this world. At this time, the famous painter Wu Yunlin bid farewell to this cruel world, leaving behind his elderly wife, his three lovely daughters, and hundreds of carefully crafted masterpieces from his lifetime, and quietly passed away. In order to mourn and commemorate this famous painter, his family members and his students opened a "Posthumous Works Exhibition" for him and sold his works. Those taking care of the scene that day, in addition to his three daughters, Jingfen (Hu Die), Ruifen (Yan Yuexian), and Shufen (Lin Li), also included his students Zhao Xuan (Zhao Dan) and Ma Yicang (Sun Min), etc. The gentlemanly student Ma Yicang (Sun Min) looked at a portrait of a beautiful woman and thought silently in his heart, "How beautiful this woman is! But it's a pity that this one is not for sale." He asked Jingfen in a low voice, "Is this photo for sale?" "Ah!" Jingfen seemed to be troubled when she heard this. After a moment of contemplation, she said, "Ah! You have to ask my mother!" "Then I'll just have to come to your house tomorrow to discuss it with your teacher's wife." The next morning, this gentlemanly college student drove an eight-cylinder Buick car to Jingfen's house. As a result of the discussion, Mother Wu was unwilling to sell it, because it was a posthumous portrait of her younger sister. But Yicang had no choice. He saw that everything in the room seemed to be messy. He tilted his head and asked very affectionately in a kind tone, "Looking at them like this, are they going to move?" Mother Wu smiled bitterly and nodded, "That's right! We don't have a house and we're in trouble!" Hearing this, Yicang turned his head to look at the beautiful three sisters and said, "Teacher's wife, it's a bit presumptuous to say this, but I wonder what you think? I have a new villa that's empty." Mother Wu was still being polite, but Yicang said again, "Don't be polite, old lady! We are teacher and student!" The "Three Sisters" also urged, "Mother, let's move!" In the end, the old woman could not resist Yicang's repeated requests and the encouragement of her three daughters, and she finally agreed. They moved into their new home. These three innocent and lively sisters were all angels in the eyes of the gentlemanly Ma Yicang, especially the quiet and gentle eldest sister Jingfen, who was the one he loved day and night in his mind. So one day he asked, "Miss Wu, can you allow me to paint a portrait of you?" Jingfen said, "I have to discuss it with my mother first!" The next day, Jingfen discussed this with her mother, and her mother agreed immediately. Rui and Shu also supported it. Suddenly, the poor boy Zhao Xuan ran over. When he heard about this, he expressed his opinion: "I still shouldn't associate with him too much! Whenever the teacher was alive, he would scold him harshly!" (To be continued) The novel "Till Seas Dry and Rocks Rot" will be suspended for a few days due to the non-arrival of the continuation.
